### SHOULD/MAY Dispositions

| Atomic ID | Primary plan | Planning-time disposition |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `N069-IMPLEMENTATION-DEPENDENCY-AND-INSTAL-B002` | `069-04` | Promoted to required: `z00z_storage::checkpoint::recursive_v2` is the sole owner of both backend adapters and verifier implementations after feasibility/predicate gates; no recursive backend crate exists. |
| `N069-IMPLEMENTATION-DEPENDENCY-AND-INSTAL-B003` | `069-09` | Conditional ownership rule: if Kubo/IPFS or archive-operator process integration is exercised, only rollup owns the RPC/process seam; storage/backend crates remain transport-free. The dependency/source audit is mandatory even when no external process is available. |
| `N069-PLONKY3-EPOCH-PROOF-CONTRACT-B006` | `069-08` | Conditional MUST: when Nova proofs exist for the epoch, `nova_chain_root` is present and binds the exact ordered proof digests; absence is allowed only for an explicitly Nova-free epoch profile. |
| `N069-MEASUREMENT-CONTRACT-B008` | `069-11` | Promoted to required: repeatable local fixtures and executed Criterion measurements are closure gates. |
| `N069-CONFIG-GATES-B075` | `069-03` | Promoted to required: checkpoint/sidecar/PQ store construction accepts the validated config handle or its versioned immutable projection; no second parser/validator is allowed. |
| `N069-MODULE-OWNERSHIP-PLAN-B001` | `069-04` | Promoted to required ordering: production backend crate creation follows successful storage-envelope, dependency, and predicate gates. |
| `N069-PROPERTY-AND-FUZZ-TESTS-P001` | `069-03` | Promoted to required family gate: all four following property/fuzz bullets execute under their atomic primary owners; a missing corpus row fails closeout. |

## 🚫 Duplicate And Drift Gates

- Primary invariant owners: `23` unique IDs, `0` duplicates, `0` missing.
- Primary acceptance owners: `42` unique IDs, `0` duplicates, `0` missing.
- Done bullets: `26` unique ordinals, `0` duplicates, `0` missing.
- Handoff items: `13` unique ordinals, `0` duplicates, `0` missing.
- Cross-plan references are secondary/regression links and must not create a
  second owner:
  - `069-03` owns predicate/context semantics; `05`, `07`, `08` implement them.
  - `069-04` owns receipt capability/construction; backends emit and the
    rollup-owned `069-09` seam converts/persists storage-owned opaque evidence.
  - `069-06` owns Nova accumulator recovery; `069-10` owns generic jobs and
    multi-artifact transaction recovery.
  - `069-03` owns cap precedence migration; `069-09` enforces write/decode caps;
    `069-11` measures observed sizes.
  - `069-08` owns epoch schemas; `069-09` integrates them.
  - `069-12` emits simulator evidence; `069-13` audits it.

## ✅ Planning Verdict

All required groups and normative obligation families have exactly one primary
plan. Execution must fail closed on any feasibility stop, missing real backend
verification, absent evidence, duplicate contract owner, or unsupported claim.
